    <li> First of all, as with many info - mercial type products, it is not going to work exactly how you see on TV. It is not going to be one sweep on your leg and all of the hair is gone.&lt;br /&gt;This will work for you, as long as:&lt;br /&gt;(1) You get the stroke down. You have to keep the no no on a pretty steady pace when you sweep an area or it will not work. Also, it works for the hair that is growing in the opposite direction you are sweeping. So, you should go over an area in both directions to catch everything. On average for me, it takes one time in one direction, one time in the opposite, and then one more time in the first direction.&lt;br /&gt;(2) The area is clean, and you either use the buffer or scrub the area after. If you have lotion, etc on, it is going to burn onto your applicator tip (I found this out the hard way) and it will mess it up. The buffer does work for me. Some of the stubble will stay behind after you sweep the area and the buffer really does help get the hair off for me.&lt;br /&gt;(3) You are consistent and dilligent. The directions say you shouldnt let the hair get much longer than stubble length. If the hair is too long, the hair will not burn off all the way. Right now, I am using it about 2x&#x27;s a week on areas that are hairier (legs, underarms). And it does work. I have used it for about 3 weeks now and I am noticing the hair coming in more sporadically and less thick. On the bikini line (which I dont shave as often as legs and underarms), I noticed a change with the first application. The hair grew back much less and finer.&lt;br /&gt;(4)Adjust the setting for the area. If you have areas that you have shaved repeatedly for a long time, the hair will be much tougher. I use the maximum setting for legs and underarms. I use the lightest setting for my face.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Speaking of face, this may not be the best thing for people with a lot of facial hair. It is much harder to get the timing of the stroke down on your face since the area is much smaller. Also, if you dont hold the skin taught and try to use it, you may pinch you skin with it, which will leave a little scab (I found this out the hard way too).&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have used every hair removal technique under the sun (waxing, threading, electrolysis, plucking, laser) and this is by far the least painful. All you will feel is warmth as you sweep the area. I have sensitive skin, and I have not broken out. With every other method I have used, I got a rash.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall,this is a good product and will work if you are dilligent and follow the directions, and if you are realistic with your expectations. Like I said before, one application is not going to leave you hair free.ht and try to use it, you may pinch you skin with it, which will leave a little scab (I found this out the hard way too).    I have used every hair removal technique under the sun (waxing, threading, electrolysis, plucking, laser) and this is by far the least painful. All you will feel is warmth as you sweep the area. I have sensitive skin, and I have not broken out. With every other method I have used, I got a rash.    Overall,this is a good product and will work if you are dilligent and follow the directions, and if you are realistic with your expectations. Like I said before, one application is not going to leave you hair free.</li>

    <li> I have purchased this and other products from TV commercials over the years and I have also done a fair amount of research on these TV products, and this is my conclusion; MOST TV products (which I call the $19.95 TV Scams) are junk, just like this. They either are made over seas and of very poor quality or do not do what they are made to do. The whole reason these products are sold over the TV and not in stores like Home Depot, Sears or Walmart is because the scammers who sell these pieces of junk are after the Shipping &amp; Handling Charges.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Ever wonder why the Shipping and handling charges are so high? They have this scam down to a science. Advertise the product, give a second unit for free, and just charge shipping &amp; handling charges for the second unit...and those S&amp;H charges are always way way high.Well it&#x27;s because that is the way they actually make their money. Now here is the scam and how it works..&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I sell you a product for 19.95 + 12.99 s&amp;h, and I give you a second unit for free + 12.99 s&amp;h. I have now gotten 25.98 in s&amp;h but I put both units in the same box and it only costs me about 10 bucks to send it to you. My profit on s&amp;h is 15.98. The product is junk and you return it. I refund you the cost of the units less the s&amp;h &#x3D; my profits are still 15.98 after everything and you are out 25.98 + the cost of shipping it back to me. I sell 800,000 of these products over the course of a year with heavy advertisements. EVEN IF EVERY BUYER RETURNS THEIR PRODUCT, I will have still made $12,784,000 on that second s&amp;h for the free unit. The products were produced overseas for a total cost of about $3.00 per unit total to my door. I had 1 million units made for a total cost of 3 mill. MY PROFITS are still $9,784,000 and even after all the other costs of advertisements and the call in &amp; delivery services, I still made millions in profit on bogus shipping and handling charges...that&#x27;s why it&#x27;s called shipping &amp; &amp;#34;HANDLING&amp;#34;.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have come to the conclusion that most of these TV sold products are sold ONLY for the shipping &amp; handling charges as a profit. Anyone can contact an overseas manufacturing company, buy a product that is made inferior to it&#x27;s competition, advertise it on TV as the best product in it&#x27;s class, or the best thing since slice bread,  and make millions on s&amp;h charges.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;DON&#x27;T BE FOOLED BY ANY $19.95 TV SCAM PRODUCTS.     <li> Regarding the No No, be sure you understand what IS and is NOT advertised/proven. My No No is (unfortunately) exactly what is advertised: a hair removal product -- period.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;You, as I, are looking for a PERMANENT hair removal product.  No No does not advertise that it will permanently remove your unwanted hair -- and it doesn&#x27;t do so.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;No No is essentially an electric shaver that burns off, as opposed to cuts off, your unwanted hair. You will want to spray air freshener after using it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;No No advertises that using it results in slower regrowth of hair. Think about this.  Hair grows at the same rate of speed whether it&#x27;s starting from below the skin or at skin level, such as when you chop it off with a razor or scissors. If you remove hair below the skin surface i.e., by tweezing, waxing or using the No No, it merely APPEARS to \\&quot;grow slower.\\&quot;  If I shave a whisker from my female chinny chin chin, its stub can be felt by bedtime.  If I pull it out, it will reappear maybe 2 days later. There&#x27;s no \\&quot;slowing\\&quot; in the GROWTH RATE of a hair plucked from my chin. Rather, there is a LENGTHENING of the time before the hair says \\&quot;Howdy do\\&quot; after a longer trip.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A positive comment about No No is that it appears to do sufficient damage to SOME hair shafts below the skin on my face and lower legs to make regrowth visible a day or two later than would be expected after shaving or using a depilatory.     <li> My Mom owns the no no hair series and it&#x27;s okay she&#x27;s been using it for a while and her hair is slowing growth. She hasn&#x27;t had hair on her upper lip for a couple months now. Now I use the pro series and I have to say I like it better than the hair series because I have some coarse hair on my chin and it gets it better then the hair series. Both the hair and pro series use the same tips so if you own this one and want to upgrade to the pro you don&#x27;t have to buy more tips right away. It&#x27;s a big plus considering the cost of refill tips. My mom after trying out my pro with her tips wants to upgrade to the pro. If you have thick hair I&#x27;d suggest the pro 5 series the hair is good for thinner and less coarse hair. It still works on it but it takes longer and the longer you have to use your tip per session the quicker it burns out. The pro series has two tips the one like the hair only it has better control it can work hotter without burning you, still work as well, get as close and last as long (unless it is a defective wire) and the then you have the pro 5 which is made for thicker coarse hair and instead of just 3 settings it has 4. The regular pro works great for me, but for my friend has thick dark coarse hair on her legs, almost like a mans beard on her legs she needs the pro 5 series and she says that it works better than razors for her it just takes longer.&lt;br /&gt;How this works is simple the tip has a little wire that heats up and burns your hair, yes you get a burnt hair smell from it and lets you know it is working. It even tells you so in the instructions so why people are complaining about it I don&#x27;t know. It&#x27;s kind of a duh your burning the hair did you expect it to smell like roses even though they tell you it burns the hair and you&#x27;re going to smell burnt hair, that&#x27;s what tells you it&#x27;s working. If you leave it like that you are going to be walking around smelling like you just walked out of a fire so you buff it. The buffer will just take off the burnt part of the hair if you go over it lightly once and leave you with annoying stubble. Go over it a few times and your legs will be smooth. The buffer is like an extra fine sandpaper and it doesn&#x27;t hurt If you have ever used a buffer instead of a razor you&#x27;ll know what you are doing, if you haven&#x27;t the videos don&#x27;t really explain it too well and you will be left with a lot of stubble like you see a lot of people complaining about.&lt;br /&gt;How to use the buffer properly press lightly and go small circular motions in a straight line up and down for like legs or side to side for like the jaw line on your face, then go back in the opposite direction rotating in the opposite direction as well so if you were going clockwise down your leg from the knee to the ankle you would go counter clockwise up your leg from the ankle to the knee. Do this until it is smooth, you may need to wipe away the dried skin and hair off the buffer and where you are doing so that it works better and faster. Then you can rinse off your legs and put on your capi slow lotion then go.&lt;br /&gt;It does take longer than shaving with a razor but it lasts longer than a razor and your legs feel smoother and not only does it grow slower the more you use it, as long as you use the lotion with capi slow, your hair gets softer as it goes. It takes longer when you are first learning to use and it gets quicker the more you use it one because your hair is less and thinner and two because you&#x27;ve learned the perfect speed and you are no longer going too fast so that it is not getting as much and having to go over it several time or going too slow and it stopping and having to start a little farther back so it gets all of it. Don&#x27;t worry it doesn&#x27;t take long to master it&#x27;s kind of like when you first learned to shave your legs with a razor.&lt;br /&gt;Tip really long hair doesn&#x27;t do so well it takes longer to get to because the plate in front that is meant to lift the hair up so the wire can burn it ends up holding it down until the wire has past so it doesn&#x27;t burn it right away. If you can trim it before hand or shave a day or two before you use it so that your hair is no more than 1/4 inch and it will go so much faster and you won&#x27;t burn out your tip as quickly by having to use it so much just to do it. Also in all honesty their buffers are not the greatest they are done after 1 or 2 uses so I got the smooth away kit from amazon (actually when you get it it is called silky smooth but is listed as smooth away) and this works much better and lasts a lot longer. I used to use smooth away all the time instead of a razor before they stopped selling them in stores in my area. Now if you have ever used a buffer instead of a razor you know that it can be time consuming and if you do it too much your skin will be red or you can have patches of hair left but using the no no first then buffing is so much faster and so much better.     <li> This no no thing is aweful if you want to remove hair permanently. I have had electrolysis and laser hair removal for over 20 years. I have PCOS and the side effects are facial hair so I will never be hair free. I bought this hoping it would work between sessions at the doctors office and it does not. The only way to stun the growth of hair is by killing the ROOT. All this thing does is burn the hair on the surface. It seems like it works because you smell the hair burning and see a light pulse which makes it seem like its getting deeper but it isnt. This is exactly the same as shaving. All you are doing is removing the surface hair and not getting the root below the skin. Depending on how fast your hair grows, all people are different, you will see the hair come right back. Do not waste your money if you want any coarse, dark hair gone for good.&lt;br /&gt;Tip: Shaving does not make your hair thicker or darker. Shaving does the same thing. It removes the hair from the surface. It does nothing to the root which is the only way that changes the appearance and texture of the hair. Hence, waxing and plucking will.</li>
    <li> I have had some facial hair since early adulthood and I have tried bleaching, waxing, tweezing, threading, laser, cream, etc. I saw an infomercial for NO NO. I paid a 1.57 for two springs and just removed the clips.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I watched the REM how-to-video and used my little 79 cent spring to remove the hair from my lip and chin while watching TV and w/o a mirror.
